SENTPOS COCA_acad_wlp_2009_03_FILE##4071262 COCA  A    0  216 <p> The findings from our study are also consistent with those from the current literature on class scheduling and spacing effects , which have confirmed that distributed ( i.e. , spaced ) practice is significantly superior to massed practice .
SENTPOS COCA_acad_wlp_2009_03_FILE##4071262 COCA  B    0  216 <p>_Y The_AT findings_NN2 from_II our_APPGE study_NN1 are_VBR also_RR consistent_JJ with_IW those_DD2 from_II the_AT current_JJ literature_NN1 on_II class_NN1 scheduling_NN1_VVG and_CC spacing_VVG_NN1 effects_NN2 ,_Y which_DDQ have_VH0 confirmed_VVN that_CST_DD1 distributed_JJ@_VVN_VVD@ (_Y i.e._REX ,_Y spaced_VVN )_Y practice_NN1 is_VBZ significantly_RR superior_JJ to_II massed_JJ practice_NN1 ._Y
SENTPOS COCA_acad_wlp_2009_03_FILE##4071262 COCA  A    0  217 For example , Smith and Rothkopf ( 1984 ) found that distributing lessons over 4 days was more effective than a single-day presentation , and that the effect of massing was primarily on the short-term retrieval of facts rather than on long-term learning .
